[2026/03/09 00:10:33] [action_start]: Running action write_file with input: {'file_path': 'scripts/yf.py', 'content': '#!/usr/bin/env python3\n"""\nStock Market Pro - Yahoo Finance data fetcher\nFast, local-first market research toolkit\n"""\n\nimport yfinance as yf\nimport argparse\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nimport matplotlib.dates as mdates\nfrom matplotlib.dates import DateFormatter\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nimport os\nimport sys\n\ndef get_price(ticker):\n    """Get current price and basic info"""\n    stock = yf.Ticker(ticker)\n    info = stock.info\n    \n    current_price = info.get(\'currentPrice\', \'N/A\')\n    previous_close = info.get(\'previousClose\', \'N/A\')\n    change = current_price - previous_close if current_price != \'N/A\' and previous_close != \'N/A\' else \'N/A\'\n    change_pct = (change / previous_close * 100) if change != \'N/A\' and previous_close != \'N/A\' else \'N/A\'\n    \n    print(f"{ticker} - Current: ${current_price:.2f}")\n    print(f"Previous Close: ${previous_close:.2f}")\n    if change != \'N/A\':\n        print(f"Change: ${change:.2f} ({change_pct:.2f}%)")\n    print(f"Volume: {info.get(\'volume\', \'N/A\'):,}")\n    print(f"Market Cap: ${info.get(\'marketCap\', 0):,}")\n\ndef get_fundamentals(ticker):\n    """Get fundamental data"""\n    stock = yf.Ticker(ticker)\n    info = stock.info\n    \n    print(f"\\n{ticker} Fundamentals:")\n    print(f"Market Cap: ${info.get(\'marketCap\', 0):,}")\n    print(f"Forward P/E: {info.get(\'forwardPE\', \'N/A\')}")\n    print(f"Trailing P/E: {info.get(\'trailingPE\', \'N/A\')}")\n    print(f"EPS: ${info.get(\'trailingEps\', \'N/A\')}")\n    print(f"Forward EPS: ${info.get(\'forwardEps\', \'N/A\')}")\n    print(f"ROE: {info.get(\'returnOnEquity\', \'N/A\')}")\n    print(f"Revenue Growth: {info.get(\'revenueGrowth\', \'N/A\')}")\n    print(f"Profit Margin: {info.get(\'profitMargins\', \'N/A\')}")\n\ndef get_history(ticker, period="1mo"):\n    """Get historical price data and show ASCII trend"""\n    stock = yf.Ticker(ticker)\n    hist = stock.history(period=period)\n    \n    if hist.empty:\n        print(f"No data found for {ticker}")\n        return\n    \n    print(f"\\n{ticker} Price History ({period}):")\n    print(f"High: ${hist[\'High\'].max():.2f}")\n    print(f"Low: ${hist[\'Low\'].min():.2f}")\n    print(f"Average Volume: {hist[\'Volume\'].mean():,.0f}")\n    \n    # Simple ASCII trend\n    recent = hist.tail(10)\n    print("\\nRecent 10-day trend:")\n    for i, (date, row) in enumerate(recent.iterrows()):\n        direction = "▲" if row[\'Close\'] > row[\'Open\'] else "▼"\n        print(f"{date.strftime(\'%m/%d\')} {direction} ${row[\'Close\']:.2f}")\n\ndef calculate_indicators(data, indicators):\n    """Calculate technical indicators"""\n    df = data.copy()\n    \n    if \'rsi\' in indicators:\n        # RSI calculation\n        delta = df[\'Close\'].diff()\n        gain = (delta.where(delta > 0, 0)).rolling(window=14).mean()\n        loss = (-delta.where(delta < 0, 0)).rolling(window=14).mean()\n        rs = gain / loss\n        df[\'RSI\'] = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    \n    if \'macd\' in indicators:\n        # MACD calculation\n        exp1 = df[\'Close\'].ewm(span=12).mean()\n        exp2 = df[\'Close\'].ewm(span=26).mean()\n        df[\'MACD\'] = exp1 - exp2\n        df[\'MACD_Signal\'] = df[\'MACD\'].ewm(span=9).mean()\n        df[\'MACD_Histogram\'] = df[\'MACD\'] - df[\'MACD_Signal\']\n    \n    if \'bb\' in indicators:\n        # Bollinger Bands\n        df[\'BB_Middle\'] = df[\'Close\'].rolling(window=20).mean()\n        bb_std = df[\'Close\'].rolling(window=20).std()\n        df[\'BB_Upper\'] = df[\'BB_Middle\'] + (bb_std * 2)\n        df[\'BB_Lower\'] = df[\'BB_Middle\'] - (bb_std * 2)\n    \n    if \'vwap\' in indicators:\n        # VWAP\n        df[\'VWAP\'] = (df[\'Volume\'] * (df[\'High\'] + df[\'Low\'] + df[\'Close\']) / 3).cumsum() / df[\'Volume\'].cumsum()\n    \n    if \'atr\' in indicators:\n        # ATR\n        df[\'TR1\'] = df[\'High\'] - df[\'Low\']\n        df[\'TR2\'] = abs(df[\'High\'] - df[\'Close\'].shift())\n        df[\'TR3\'] = abs(df[\'Low\'] - df[\'Close\'].shift())\n        df[\'True_Range\'] = df[[\'TR1\', \'TR2\', \'TR3\']].max(axis=1)\n        df[\'ATR\'] = df[\'True_Range\'].rolling(window=14).mean()\n    \n    return df\n\ndef create_pro_chart(ticker, period="6mo", chart_type="candlestick", indicators=None):\n    """Create professional chart with indicators"""\n    if indicators is None:\n        indicators = []\n    \n    stock = yf.Ticker(ticker)\n    data = stock.history(period=period)\n    \n    if data.empty:\n        print(f"No data found for {ticker}")\n        return None\n    \n    # Calculate indicators\n    data = calculate_indicators(data, indicators)\n    \n    # Create figure with subplots for indicators\n    rows = 1 + len([i for i in indicators if i in [\'rsi\', \'macd\', \'atr\']])\n    fig, axes = plt.subplots(rows, 1, figsize=(12, 4 * rows), sharex=True)\n    \n    if rows == 1:\n        axes = [axes]\n    \n    # Main price chart\n    ax = axes[0]\n    \n    if chart_type == "line":\n        ax.plot(data.index, data[\'Close\'], label=\'Close Price\', linewidth=2)\n    else:\n        # Candlestick chart\n        ax.plot(data.index, data[\'Close\'], label=\'Close Price\', alpha=0.7)\n        # Simple candlestick representation\n        for i, (date, row) in enumerate(data.iterrows()):\n            color = \'green\' if row[\'Close\'] > row[\'Open\'] else \'red\'\n            ax.plot([date, date], [row[\'Low\'], row[\'High\']], color=\'black\', linewidth=1)\n            ax.plot([date, date], [row[\'Open\'], row[\'Close\']], color=color, linewidth=3)\n    \n    # Add indicators to main chart\n    if \'bb\' in indicators:\n        ax.plot(data.index, data[\'BB_Upper\'], \'r--\', alpha=0.7, label=\'BB Upper\')\n        ax.plot(data.index, data[\'BB_Lower\'], \'r--\', alpha=0.7, label=\'BB Lower\')\n        ax.fill_between(data.index, data[\'BB_Upper\'], data[\'BB_Lower\'], alpha=0.1, color=\'gray\')\n    \n    if \'vwap\' in indicators:\n        ax.plot(data.index, data[\'VWAP\'], \'purple\', alpha=0.7, label=\'VWAP\')\n    \n    ax.set_title(f\'{ticker} - {period} Chart\')\n    ax.set_ylabel(\'Price ($)\')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n    \n    # Add RSI subplot\n    current_row = 1\n    if \'rsi\' in indicators and current_row < len(axes):\n        ax_rsi = axes[current_row]\n        ax_rsi.plot(data.index, data[\'RSI\'], \'blue\', label=\'RSI\')\n        ax_rsi.axhline(y=70, color=\'r\', linestyle=\'--\', alpha=0.7, label=\'Overbought (70)\')\n        ax_rsi.axhline(y=30, color=\'g\', linestyle=\'--\', alpha=0.7, label=\'Oversold (30)\')\n        ax_rsi.set_ylabel(\'RSI\')\n        ax_rsi.legend()\n        ax_rsi.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n        current_row += 1\n    \n    # Add MACD subplot\n    if \'macd\' in indicators and current_row < len(axes):\n        ax_macd = axes[current_row]\n        ax_macd.plot(data.index, data[\'MACD\'], \'blue\', label=\'MACD\')\n        ax_macd.plot(data.index, data[\'MACD_Signal\'], \'red\', label=\'Signal\')\n        ax_macd.bar(data.index, data[\'MACD_Histogram\'], alpha=0.3, label=\'Histogram\')\n        ax_macd.set_ylabel(\'MACD\')\n        ax_macd.legend()\n        ax_macd.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n        current_row += 1\n    \n    # Add ATR subplot\n    if \'atr\' in indicators and current_row < len(axes):\n        ax_atr = axes[current_row]\n        ax_atr.plot(data.index, data[\'ATR\'], \'orange\', label=\'ATR\')\n        ax_atr.set_ylabel(\'ATR\')\n        ax_atr.legend()\n        ax_atr.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n    \n    # Format x-axis\n    axes[-1].xaxis.set_major_formatter(DateFormatter(\'%Y-%m-%d\'))\n    axes[-1].xaxis.set_major_locator(mdates.MonthLocator())\n    plt.xticks(rotation=45)\n    \n    plt.tight_layout()\n    \n    # Save chart\n    chart_path = f"/tmp/{ticker}_{period}_pro_chart.png"\n    plt.savefig(chart_path, dpi=300, bbox_inches=\'tight\')\n    plt.close()\n    \n    print(f"Chart saved: {chart_path}")\n    return chart_path\n\ndef generate_report(ticker, period="6mo"):\n    """Generate comprehensive report"""\n    print(f"\\n=== {ticker} Stock Analysis Report ===\\n")\n    \n    # Get current price\n    get_price(ticker)\n    print()\n    \n    # Get fundamentals\n    get_fundamentals(ticker)\n    print()\n    \n    # Get recent history\n    get_history(ticker, "1mo")\n    print()\n    \n    # Generate chart with common indicators\n    chart_path = create_pro_chart(ticker, period, indicators=[\'rsi\', \'macd\', \'bb\'])\n    \n    print(f"\\nTechnical Analysis Summary:")\n    print(f"Chart generated: {chart_path}")\n    \n    # Simple forecast based on recent trend\n    stock = yf.Ticker(ticker)\n    hist = stock.history(period="1mo")\n    \n    if not hist.empty:\n        recent_trend = (hist[\'Close\'].iloc[-1] - hist[\'Close\'].iloc[-5]) / hist[\'Close\'].iloc[-5] * 100\n        volatility = hist[\'Close\'].pct_change().std() * np.sqrt(252) * 100\n        \n        print(f"Recent 5-day trend: {recent_trend:.2f}%")\n        print(f"Annualized volatility: {volatility:.1f}%")\n        \n        # Simple forecast (this is not financial advice!)\n        current_price = hist[\'Close\'].iloc[-1]\n        forecast_range = current_price * (volatility / 100 / np.sqrt(52))  # Weekly volatility\n        \n        print(f"\\nNext Week Price Forecast (based on volatility):")\n        print(f"Expected range: ${current_price - forecast_range:.2f} - ${current_price + forecast_range:.2f}")\n        print(f"Current price: ${current_price:.2f}")\n    \n    return chart_path\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description=\'Stock Market Pro - Yahoo Finance Tool\')\n    parser.add_argument(\'command\', choices=[\'price\', \'fundamentals\', \'history\', \'pro\', \'chart\', \'report\', \'option\'])\n    parser.add_argument(\'ticker\', help=\'Stock ticker symbol\')\n    parser.add_argument(\'period\', nargs=\'?\', default=\'6mo\', [2026/03/09 01:47:23] [agent message]: Based on my research, here's comprehensive information about the IPSJ conference:

**What IPSJ Stands For:**
IPSJ stands for "Information Processing Society of Japan" (Japanese: 情報処理学会)

**Organization Overview:**
- Founded: April 22, 1960 (over 64 years ago)
- Headquarters: Tokyo, Japan
- Membership: Nearly 20,000 members (including regular, student, and corporate members)
- Status: Largest and leading information technology society in Japan
- International Affiliation: Full member of the International Federation for Information Processing (IFIP)

**Purpose and Mission:**
IPSJ serves as the leading authority in technical areas of information processing and computer science for professionals and students. The society plays a key role in realizing the information society of the 21st century through its academic, cultural, and industrial activities. Their mission is to provide leadership for the sound evolution of computer science and technology in an increasingly computerized society.

**Conferences and Events:**
IPSJ organizes and sponsors various conferences and workshops, including:

1. **Annual National Convention**: Their flagship event (recently held the 87th annual convention on March 14, 2025)
2. **International Conferences**: Including events like COMPSAC and ASP-DAC
3. **Special Interest Group (SIG) Conferences**: Various specialized conferences on specific topics
4. **Programming Symposium**: Regular technical symposiums
5. **Software Japan**: Software-focused events
6. **AI Programming Contests**: Including "SamurAI coding" competitions

**Topics Covered:**
IPSJ conferences cover a wide range of information processing and computer science topics, including:
- Programming and software development
- Database systems
- Human-computer interaction
- Ubiquitous computing
- Computer vision and applications
- Bioinformatics
- Digital contents and media
- System design and LSI methodology
- Consumer devices and systems
- Mathematical modeling

**Publications:**
The society publishes several academic journals and magazines, including:
- Joho Shori magazine
- Journal of Information Processing
- Multiple peer-reviewed transactions on specialized topics
- IPSJ Online Transactions (open access)

**When and Where:**
- Main annual convention: Typically held in March each year
- Various international conferences: Held throughout the year in different locations (Tokyo, Osaka, etc.)
- Headquarters: Tokyo, Japan

**Additional Features:**
- Maintains an online Computer Museum documenting Japanese computer development
- Has inducted Japanese Fellows annually since 1999
- Provides various membership categories for professionals, students, and organizations

The IPSJ is a major academic and professional organization that serves as Japan's primary society for computing and information processing, playing a crucial role in advancing computer science research and education in Japan and internationally.

3 Month View\', fontsize=16, fontweight=\'bold\')\n\n# Chart 1: Price and Moving Averages\nax1.plot(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Close\'], label=\'Close Price\', linewidth=2, color=\'black\')\nax1.plot(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(20).mean(), label=\'20-day MA\', alpha=0.7, color=\'blue\')\nax1.plot(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(50).mean(), label=\'50-day MA\', alpha=0.7, color=\'red\')\nax1.set_title(\'Price with Moving Averages\')\nax1.set_ylabel(\'Price ($)\')\nax1.legend()\nax1.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n# Chart 2: Bollinger Bands\nbb_middle = hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(20).mean()\nbb_upper = bb_middle + (hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(20).std() * 2)\nbb_lower = bb_middle - (hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(20).std() * 2)\n\nax2.plot(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Close\'], label=\'Close Price\', color=\'black\', linewidth=2)\nax2.plot(hist_3mo.index, bb_upper, label=\'Upper Band\', color=\'green\', alpha=0.7)\nax2.plot(hist_3mo.index, bb_middle, label=\'Middle Band\', color=\'blue\', alpha=0.7)\nax2.plot(hist_3mo.index, bb_lower, label=\'Lower Band\', color=\'red\', alpha=0.7)\nax2.fill_between(hist_3mo.index, bb_upper, bb_lower, alpha=0.1, color=\'gray\')\nax2.set_title(\'Bollinger Bands (20-day)\')\nax2.set_ylabel(\'Price ($)\')\nax2.legend()\nax2.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n# Chart 3: RSI\ndef calculate_rsi_series(prices, window=14):\n    delta = prices.diff()\n    gain = (delta.where(delta > 0, 0)).rolling(window=window).mean()\n    loss = (-delta.where(delta < 0, 0)).rolling(window=window).mean()\n    rs = gain / loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\nrsi = calculate_rsi_series(hist_3mo[\'Close\'])\nax3.plot(hist_3mo.index, rsi, color=\'purple\', linewidth=2)\nax3.axhline(y=70, color=\'red\', linestyle=\'--\', alpha=0.7, label=\'Overbought (70)\')\nax3.axhline(y=30, color=\'green\', linestyle=\'--\', alpha=0.7, label=\'Oversold (30)\')\nax3.axhline(y=50, color=\'gray\', linestyle=\'-\', alpha=0.5)\nax3.set_title(\'RSI (14-day)\')\nax3.set_ylabel(\'RSI\')\nax3.set_ylim(0, 100)\nax3.legend()\nax3.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n# Chart 4: Volume\nax4.bar(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Volume\'], alpha=0.7, color=\'orange\', width=1)\nax4.set_title(\'Volume\')\nax4.set_ylabel(\'Volume\')\nax4.set_xlabel(\'Date\')\nax4.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n# Format x-axis for all charts\nfor ax in [ax1, ax2, ax3, ax4]:\n    ax.xaxis.set_major_formatter(mdates.DateFormatter(\'%m/%d\'))\n    ax.xaxis.set_major_locator(mdates.WeekdayLocator(interval=2))\n    plt.setp(ax.xaxis.get_majorticklabels(), rotation=45)\n\nplt.tight_layout()\n\n# Save the chart\nchart_path = \'workspace/amd_technical_analysis.png\'\nplt.savefig(chart_path, dpi=300, bbox_inches=\'tight\')\nplt.show()\n\nprint(f"Technical analysis chart saved to: {chart_path}")\nprint(f"Chart shows 3-month view with moving averages, Bollinger Bands, RSI, and volume analysis")', '_session_id': 'b0494611-f969-4865-a651-410caee171c0'}.

3 Month View\', fontsize=16, fontweight=\'bold\')\n\n# Chart 1: Price and Moving Averages\nax1.plot(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Close\'], label=\'Close Price\', linewidth=2, color=\'black\')\nax1.plot(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(20).mean(), label=\'20-day MA\', alpha=0.7, color=\'blue\')\nax1.plot(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(50).mean(), label=\'50-day MA\', alpha=0.7, color=\'red\')\nax1.set_title(\'Price with Moving Averages\')\nax1.set_ylabel(\'Price ($)\')\nax1.legend()\nax1.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n# Chart 2: Bollinger Bands\nbb_middle = hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(20).mean()\nbb_upper = bb_middle + (hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(20).std() * 2)\nbb_lower = bb_middle - (hist_3mo[\'Close\'].rolling(20).std() * 2)\n\nax2.plot(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Close\'], label=\'Close Price\', color=\'black\', linewidth=2)\nax2.plot(hist_3mo.index, bb_upper, label=\'Upper Band\', color=\'green\', alpha=0.7)\nax2.plot(hist_3mo.index, bb_middle, label=\'Middle Band\', color=\'blue\', alpha=0.7)\nax2.plot(hist_3mo.index, bb_lower, label=\'Lower Band\', color=\'red\', alpha=0.7)\nax2.fill_between(hist_3mo.index, bb_upper, bb_lower, alpha=0.1, color=\'gray\')\nax2.set_title(\'Bollinger Bands (20-day)\')\nax2.set_ylabel(\'Price ($)\')\nax2.legend()\nax2.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n# Chart 3: RSI\ndef calculate_rsi_series(prices, window=14):\n    delta = prices.diff()\n    gain = (delta.where(delta > 0, 0)).rolling(window=window).mean()\n    loss = (-delta.where(delta < 0, 0)).rolling(window=window).mean()\n    rs = gain / loss\n    rsi = 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))\n    return rsi\n\nrsi = calculate_rsi_series(hist_3mo[\'Close\'])\nax3.plot(hist_3mo.index, rsi, color=\'purple\', linewidth=2)\nax3.axhline(y=70, color=\'red\', linestyle=\'--\', alpha=0.7, label=\'Overbought (70)\')\nax3.axhline(y=30, color=\'green\', linestyle=\'--\', alpha=0.7, label=\'Oversold (30)\')\nax3.axhline(y=50, color=\'gray\', linestyle=\'-\', alpha=0.5)\nax3.set_title(\'RSI (14-day)\')\nax3.set_ylabel(\'RSI\')\nax3.set_ylim(0, 100)\nax3.legend()\nax3.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n# Chart 4: Volume\nax4.bar(hist_3mo.index, hist_3mo[\'Volume\'], alpha=0.7, color=\'orange\', width=1)\nax4.set_title(\'Volume\')\nax4.set_ylabel(\'Volume\')\nax4.set_xlabel(\'Date\')\nax4.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n# Format x-axis for all charts\nfor ax in [ax1, ax2, ax3, ax4]:\n    ax.xaxis.set_major_formatter(mdates.DateFormatter(\'%m/%d\'))\n    ax.xaxis.set_major_locator(mdates.WeekdayLocator(interval=2))\n    plt.setp(ax.xaxis.get_majorticklabels(), rotation=45)\n\nplt.tight_layout()\n\n# Save the chart\nimport os\nos.makedirs(\'workspace\', exist_ok=True)\nchart_path = \'workspace/amd_technical_analysis.png\'\nplt.savefig(chart_path, dpi=300, bbox_inches=\'tight\')\nplt.close()\n\nprint(f"Technical analysis chart saved to: {chart_path}")\nprint(f"Chart shows 3-month view with moving averages, Bollinger Bands, RSI, and volume analysis")', '_session_id': 'b0494611-f969-4865-a651-410caee171c0'}.
